\DoxyCodeLine{02499\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02500\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02501\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02502\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02503\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02504\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ A\ list\ of\ bit-\/field\ constants\ used\ with\ @FT\_Load\_Glyph\ to\ indicate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02505\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ what\ kind\ of\ operations\ to\ perform\ during\ glyph\ loading.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02506\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02507\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02508\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_DEFAULT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02509\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Corresponding\ to\string~0,\ this\ value\ is\ used\ as\ the\ default\ glyph\ load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02510\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ operation.\ \ In\ this\ case,\ the\ following\ happens:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02511\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02512\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 1.\ FreeType\ looks\ for\ a\ bitmap\ for\ the\ glyph\ corresponding\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02513\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ face's\ current\ size.\ \ If\ one\ is\ found,\ the\ function\ returns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02514\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ bitmap\ data\ can\ be\ accessed\ from\ the\ glyph\ slot\ (see\ note}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02515\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02516\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02517\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 2.\ If\ no\ embedded\ bitmap\ is\ searched\ or\ found,\ FreeType\ looks\ for\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02518\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scalable\ outline.\ \ If\ one\ is\ found,\ it\ is\ loaded\ from\ the\ font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02519\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ file,\ scaled\ to\ device\ pixels,\ then\ \`{}hinted'\ to\ the\ pixel\ grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02520\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ in\ order\ to\ optimize\ it.\ \ The\ outline\ data\ can\ be\ accessed\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02521\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ glyph\ slot\ (see\ note\ below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02522\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02523\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ by\ default,\ the\ glyph\ loader\ doesn't\ render\ outlines\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02524\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmaps.\ \ The\ following\ flags\ are\ used\ to\ modify\ this\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02525\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ behaviour\ to\ more\ specific\ and\ useful\ cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02526\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02527\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02528\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Don't\ scale\ the\ loaded\ outline\ glyph\ but\ keep\ it\ in\ font\ units.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02529\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02530\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ implies\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING\ and\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP,\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02531\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ unsets\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02532\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02533\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ If\ the\ font\ is\ \`{}tricky'\ (see\ @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_TRICKY\ for\ more),\ using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02534\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ usually\ yields\ meaningless\ outlines\ because\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02535\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ subglyphs\ must\ be\ scaled\ and\ positioned\ with\ hinting\ instructions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02536\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ can\ be\ solved\ by\ loading\ the\ font\ without\ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02537\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ setting\ the\ character\ size\ to\ \`{}font-\/>units\_per\_EM'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02538\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02539\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02540\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Disable\ hinting.\ \ This\ generally\ generates\ \`{}blurrier'\ bitmap\ glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02541\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ when\ the\ glyph\ are\ rendered\ in\ any\ of\ the\ anti-\/aliased\ modes.\ \ See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02542\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ also\ the\ note\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02543\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02544\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ implied\ by\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02545\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02546\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Call\ @FT\_Render\_Glyph\ after\ the\ glyph\ is\ loaded.\ \ By\ default,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ glyph\ is\ rendered\ in\ @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL\ mode.\ \ This\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ overridden\ by\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX\ or\ @FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ unset\ by\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02552\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02554\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Ignore\ bitmap\ strikes\ when\ loading.\ \ Bitmap-\/only\ fonts\ ignore\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02555\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02556\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02557\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ always\ sets\ this\ flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_VERTICAL\_LAYOUT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02560\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Load\ the\ glyph\ for\ vertical\ text\ layout.\ \ In\ particular,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02561\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \`{}advance'\ value\ in\ the\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ structure\ is\ set\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02562\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \`{}vertAdvance'\ value\ of\ the\ \`{}metrics'\ field.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02563\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02564\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ In\ case\ @FT\_HAS\_VERTICAL\ doesn't\ return\ true,\ you\ shouldn't\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02565\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ this\ flag\ currently.\ \ Reason\ is\ that\ in\ this\ case\ vertical\ metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02566\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ get\ synthesized,\ and\ those\ values\ are\ not\ always\ consistent\ across}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02567\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ various\ font\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02568\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02569\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02570\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Indicates\ that\ the\ auto-\/hinter\ is\ preferred\ over\ the\ font's\ native}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02571\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ hinter.\ \ See\ also\ the\ note\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02572\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02573\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_PEDANTIC\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02574\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Indicates\ that\ the\ font\ driver\ should\ perform\ pedantic\ verifications}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02575\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ during\ glyph\ loading.\ \ This\ is\ mostly\ used\ to\ detect\ broken\ glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02576\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ in\ fonts.\ \ By\ default,\ FreeType\ tries\ to\ handle\ broken\ fonts\ also.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02577\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02578\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ In\ particular,\ errors\ from\ the\ TrueType\ bytecode\ engine\ are\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02579\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ passed\ to\ the\ application\ if\ this\ flag\ is\ not\ set;\ this\ might}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02580\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ result\ in\ partially\ hinted\ or\ distorted\ glyphs\ in\ case\ a\ glyph's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02581\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bytecode\ is\ buggy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02582\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02583\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_RECURSE\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02584\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Indicate\ that\ the\ font\ driver\ should\ not\ load\ composite\ glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02585\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ recursively.\ \ Instead,\ it\ should\ set\ the\ \`{}num\_subglyph'\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02586\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \`{}subglyphs'\ values\ of\ the\ glyph\ slot\ accordingly,\ and\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02587\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \`{}glyph-\/>format'\ to\ @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_COMPOSITE.\ \ The\ description\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02588\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ subglyphs\ can\ then\ be\ accessed\ with\ @FT\_Get\_SubGlyph\_Info.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02589\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02590\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ implies\ @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE\ and\ @FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02591\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02592\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02593\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Indicates\ that\ the\ transform\ matrix\ set\ by\ @FT\_Set\_Transform\ should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02594\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ be\ ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02595\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02596\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02597\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ used\ with\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ to\ indicate\ that\ you\ want\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02598\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ render\ an\ outline\ glyph\ to\ a\ 1-\/bit\ monochrome\ bitmap\ glyph,\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02599\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ 8\string~pixels\ packed\ into\ each\ byte\ of\ the\ bitmap\ data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02600\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02601\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ this\ has\ no\ effect\ on\ the\ hinting\ algorithm\ used.\ \ You}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02602\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ should\ rather\ use\ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO\ so\ that\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02603\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ monochrome-\/optimized\ hinting\ algorithm\ is\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02604\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02605\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_LINEAR\_DESIGN\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02606\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Indicates\ that\ the\ \`{}linearHoriAdvance'\ and\ \`{}linearVertAdvance'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02607\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ fields\ of\ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ should\ be\ kept\ in\ font\ units.\ \ See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02608\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_GlyphSlotRec\ for\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02609\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02610\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_NO\_AUTOHINT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02611\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Disable\ auto-\/hinter.\ \ See\ also\ the\ note\ below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02612\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02613\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_COLOR\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02614\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ flag\ is\ used\ to\ request\ loading\ of\ color\ embedded-\/bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02615\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ images.\ \ The\ resulting\ color\ bitmaps,\ if\ available,\ will\ have\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02616\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_BGRA\ format.\ \ When\ the\ flag\ is\ not\ used\ and\ color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02617\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmaps\ are\ found,\ they\ will\ be\ converted\ to\ 256-\/level\ gray}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02618\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ bitmaps\ transparently.\ \ Those\ bitmaps\ will\ be\ in\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02619\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_GRAY\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02620\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02621\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_CROP\_BITMAP\ ::}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02623\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02625\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Ignored.\ \ Deprecated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02626\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02627\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02628\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ By\ default,\ hinting\ is\ enabled\ and\ the\ font's\ native\ hinter\ (see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02629\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_HINTER)\ is\ preferred\ over\ the\ auto-\/hinter.\ \ You\ can}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02634\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02692\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02693\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ This\ corresponds\ to\ the\ default\ hinting\ algorithm,\ optimized\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02694\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ standard\ gray-\/level\ rendering.\ \ For\ monochrome\ output,\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ A\ lighter\ hinting\ algorithm\ for\ non-\/monochrome\ modes.\ \ Many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ generated\ glyphs\ are\ more\ fuzzy\ but\ better\ resemble\ its\ original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ shape.\ \ A\ bit\ like\ rendering\ on\ Mac\ OS\string~X.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02702\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ As\ a\ special\ exception,\ this\ target\ implies\ @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02703\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02704\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO\ ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02705\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Strong\ hinting\ algorithm\ that\ should\ only\ be\ used\ for\ monochrome}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02706\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ output.\ \ The\ result\ is\ probably\ unpleasant\ if\ the\ glyph\ is\ rendered}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02707\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ in\ non-\/monochrome\ modes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02708\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02712\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02720\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02721\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ If\ @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER\ is\ also\ set,\ the\ glyph\ is\ rendered\ in\ the}}
